   261  // CreateCustomAllocationRule Create custom allocation rule.
   262  // Create a new custom allocation rule with the specified filters and allocation strategy.
   263  //
   264  // **Strategy Methods:**
   265  // - **PROPORTIONAL/EVEN**: Allocates costs proportionally/evenly based on existing costs. Requires: granularity, allocated_by_tag_keys. Optional: based_on_costs, allocated_by_filters, evaluate_grouped_by_tag_keys, evaluate_grouped_by_filters.
   266  // - **PROPORTIONAL_TIMESERIES/EVEN_TIMESERIES**: Allocates based on timeseries data. Requires: granularity, based_on_timeseries. Optional: evaluate_grouped_by_tag_keys.
   267  // - **PERCENT**: Allocates fixed percentages to specific tags. Requires: allocated_by (array of percentage allocations).
   268  //
   269  // **Filter Conditions:**
   270  // - Use **value** for single-value conditions: "is", "is not", "contains", "=", "!=", "like", "not like"
   271  // - Use **values** for multi-value conditions: "in", "not in"
   272  // - Cannot use both value and values simultaneously.
   273  //
   274  // **Supported operators**: is, is not, contains, in, not in, =, !=, like, not like

  5290  // Reorder custom allocation rules - Change the execution order of custom allocation rules.
  5291  //
  5292  // **Important**: You must provide the **complete list** of all rule IDs in the desired execution order. The API will reorder ALL rules according to the provided sequence.
  5293  //

  5805  // UpdateCustomAllocationRule Update custom allocation rule.
  5806  // Update an existing custom allocation rule with new filters and allocation strategy.
  5807  //
  5808  // **Strategy Methods:**
  5809  // - **PROPORTIONAL/EVEN**: Allocates costs proportionally/evenly based on existing costs. Requires: granularity, allocated_by_tag_keys. Optional: based_on_costs, allocated_by_filters, evaluate_grouped_by_tag_keys, evaluate_grouped_by_filters.
  5810  // - **PROPORTIONAL_TIMESERIES/EVEN_TIMESERIES**: Allocates based on timeseries data. Requires: granularity, based_on_timeseries. Optional: evaluate_grouped_by_tag_keys.
  5811  // - **PERCENT**: Allocates fixed percentages to specific tags. Requires: allocated_by (array of percentage allocations).
  5812  // - **USAGE_METRIC**: Allocates based on usage metrics (implementation varies).
  5813  //
  5814  // **Filter Conditions:**
